25:T33d5,<entryFree id="n27712" key="ظَهَرَ" type="main">     
                  <form>       
                     <itype>1</itype>        
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">ظَهَرَ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ذ</orth>
                  </form>, (S, Msb, K, &amp;c.,) aor.      
    <form n="infl">       
                     <orth orig="Ba" lang="ar">ظَهَرَ</orth>
                  </form>, (Msb,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">ظُهُورٌ</foreign>, (S, Mgh, Msb, K, &amp;c.,) [<hi rend="ital">It was,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">became, outward, exterior, external, extrinsic,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">exoteric:</hi> and hence,] <hi rend="ital">it appeared; became apparent, overt, open, perceptible</hi> or <hi rend="ital">perceived, manifest, plain,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">evident;</hi> (S, Mgh, Msb, K, TA;) <hi rend="ital">after having been concealed,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">latent:</hi> (Msb, TA:) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n27712-1" target="تظاهر" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n27715"/></foreign> signifies the same. (Har p. 85.) Hence the phrase <foreign lang="ar">ظَهَرَ لِى رَأْىٌ</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  [<hi rend="ital">An idea,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">opinion, occurred to me</hi>], said when one knows what he did not know before. (Msb.) [And <foreign lang="ar">هٰذَا مَا يَظْهَرُ لِى</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">This is what appears to me</hi> to be the case, or to be the right way or course; or <hi rend="ital">this is my opinion.</hi>] <foreign lang="ar">ظَهَرَ الحَمْلُ</foreign>, inf. n. as above, means <hi rend="ital">Pregnancy became apparent,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">manifest:</hi> it is said that this is not the case in less than three months. (Msb.) And it is said in a trad. of 'Áïsheh, <foreign lang="ar">كَانَ يُصَلِّى العَصْرَ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">فِى حُجْرَتِى قَبْلَ أَنْ تَظْهَرَ</foreign> i. e. [<hi rend="ital">He used to perform the prayer of the afternoon in my chamber</hi>] <hi rend="ital">before it</hi> (meaning the sun) <hi rend="ital">became high and apparent:</hi> (TA:) or <foreign lang="ar">وَالشَّمْسُ فِى حُجْرَتِى لَمْ تَظْهَرْ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">بَعْدُ</foreign> i. e. [<hi rend="ital">when the sun was in my chamber,</hi>] <hi rend="ital">it not having risen high</hi> so as to be on the flat roof [thereof]: referring to the Prophet. (O. [But <foreign lang="ar">العَصْرَ</foreign> must be a mistranscription for <foreign lang="ar">الفَجْرَ</foreign>, i. e. <hi rend="ital">the prayer of the dawn.</hi>]) The saying in the Kur [xxiv. 31], <foreign lang="ar">وَلَا يُبْدِينَ زِينَتَهُنَّ إِلَّا مَا ظَهَرَ مِنْهَا</foreign> [which is app. best rendered <hi rend="ital">And that they discover not their ornature except what is external thereof</hi>] has been expl. in seven different ways, most correctly as meaning the clothes: (O, TA:) accord. to 'Áïsheh, it means the bracelet (<foreign lang="ar">القُلْب</foreign>) and the ring (<foreign lang="ar">الفَتَخَة</foreign>): and accord. to I'Ab, the hand and the signet-ring and the face. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  Also <hi rend="ital">He went forth,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">out,</hi> (Mgh, TA,) <hi rend="ital">to the outside of a place.</hi> (O, TA.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  And <hi rend="ital">He</hi> (a bird) <hi rend="ital">migrated,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">went down,</hi> from one country or region to another: used in this sense by AHn in relation to the vulture, migrating to Nejd. (L.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">ظَهَرَ عَنْهُ</foreign>, said of a vice, or fault, (O, TA,) or a disgrace, (JK, A, O,) <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">It did not cleave to him;</hi> (A, O, TA;) <hi rend="ital">it was remote from him;</hi> (TA;) <hi rend="ital">it quitted him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">departed from him.</hi> (JK.)          <sense type="b" n="5">-b5-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">ظَهَرْتُ بِهِ</foreign>, (O, TA,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">ظَهْرٌ</foreign>, (K,) <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">I gloried,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">boasted, by reason of it.</hi> (O, K * TA.) [Respecting a meaning assigned to <foreign lang="ar">ظَهَرَ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">بِفُلَانٍ</foreign> in the K, see 4.]          <sense type="b" n="6">-b6-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">أَكَلَ الرَّجُلُ أُكْلَةً</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">ظَهَرَ مِنْهَا ظَهْرَةً</foreign> means <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  [<hi rend="ital">The man ate some food</hi>] <hi rend="ital">in consequence of which</hi>] <hi rend="ital">he became fat.</hi> (TA.)       <sense type="A" n="2">-A2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">ظَهَرَهُ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">He mounted it; went,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">got, upon it,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">upon the top of it;</hi> (S, A, * Mgh, O, Msb, K;) as also <foreign lang="ar">ظَهَرَ عَلَيْهِ</foreign>; (O;) namely, a house, (S,) or a house-top, (A, Mgh, O,) and a mountain, (A,) and a wall; (O, Msb;) properly, <hi rend="ital">he became upon its back:</hi> (Mgh:) and [in like manner] one says, <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n27712-2" target="ظَهَّرَ" n="2" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar" select="n27712-1"/>فُلَانٌ نَجْدًا</foreign>, inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">تَظْهِيرٌ</foreign>, <hi rend="ital">Such a one mounted,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">went up, upon the high region</hi> (<foreign lang="ar">ظَهْر</foreign>) <hi rend="ital">of Nejd.</hi> (O.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  Hence, (Mgh, Msb,) <foreign lang="ar">ظَهَرَ عَلَيْهِ</foreign> (S, Mgh, O, Msb, K) and <foreign lang="ar">بِهِ</foreign>, (K,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">ظُهُورٌ</foreign> (Bd in xxiv. 31) and <foreign lang="ar">ظَهْرٌ</foreign> also, (Ham p. 301,) <hi rend="ital">He overcame, conquered, subdued, overpowered,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">mastered, him; gained the mastery</hi> or <hi rend="ital">victory,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">prevailed, over him;</hi> (S, Mgh, O, Msb, K;) namely, his enemy; (Msb;) and in like manner, [<hi rend="ital">he conquered, won, achieved,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">attained, it,</hi> i. e.] a thing. (O, TA.) [The saying <foreign lang="ar">فُلَانٌ لَا يَظْهَرُ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">عَلَيْهِ أَحَدٌ</foreign> is expl. in the L and TA by the words <foreign lang="ar">اى لا يَسْلَم</foreign>, and said to be tropical: but Ibr D thinks that the correct reading is <foreign lang="ar">لا يُسَلِّمُ</foreign>, from <foreign lang="ar">التَّسْلِيمُ</foreign>; and that it is said of one who will not give up, or resign, what is in his hand; so that the meaning is, <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">Such a one is a person whom no one will overcome in respect of that which he holds in his possession.</hi>]          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  And [hence also] <foreign lang="ar">ظَهَرَ عَلَيْهِ</foreign>, (Msb, TA,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">ظُهُورٌ</foreign>, (TA,) <hi rend="ital">He knew, became acquainted with,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">got knowledge of, him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it.</hi> (Msb, TA.) So in the Kur xxiv. 31, <foreign lang="ar">وَٱلطِّفْلُ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">ٱلَّذِينَ لَمْ يَظْهَرُوا عَلَى عَوْرَاتِ ٱلنِّسَآءِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">And the young children</hi>] <hi rend="ital">who have not attained knowledge of the</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">عورات</foreign>, (Bd, Jel,) meaning [<hi rend="ital">pudenda,</hi> or] <hi rend="ital">parts between the navel and the knee,</hi> (Jel,) <hi rend="ital">of women,</hi> by reason of their want of discrimination: (Bd:) or <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">who have not attained to the generative faculty;</hi> (O, Bd, * TA;) from <foreign lang="ar">الظُّهُورُ</foreign> in the sense of <foreign lang="ar">الغَلَبَةُ</foreign>. (Bd.) So too in the Kur [xviii. 19], <foreign lang="ar">إِنْ يَظْهَرُوا عَلَيْكُمْ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">If they get knowledge of you.</hi> (O, TA.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  And [hence] <foreign lang="ar">ظَهَرَ عَلَيْهِ</foreign>, (Fr, A, O, TA,) and
